2025-07-02T16:33:50.4572072Z ### Chat
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4572160Z 
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4572617Z There are 3 ways to chat with [CodeRabbit](https://coderabbit.ai?utm_source=oss&utm_medium=github&utm_campaign=ThomasJButler/The-Matrix-Arcade&utm_content=5):
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4573124Z 
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4573333Z - Review comments: Directly reply to a review comment made by CodeRabbit. Example:
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4573757Z   - `I pushed a fix in commit <commit_id>, please review it.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4574058Z   - `Explain this complex logic.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4574327Z   - `Open a follow-up GitHub issue for this discussion.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4575477Z - Files and specific lines of code (under the "Files changed" tab): Tag `@coderabbitai` in a new review comment at the desired location with your query. Examples:
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4576082Z   - `@coderabbitai explain this code block.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4576354Z   -	`@coderabbitai modularize this function.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4577072Z - PR comments: Tag `@coderabbitai` in a new PR comment to ask questions about the PR branch. For the best results, please provide a very specific query, as very limited context is provided in this mode. Examples:
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4578165Z   - `@coderabbitai gather interesting stats about this repository and render them as a table. Additionally, render a pie chart showing the language distribution in the codebase.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4578873Z   - `@coderabbitai read src/utils.ts and explain its main purpose.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4579475Z   - `@coderabbitai read the files in the src/scheduler package and generate a class diagram using mermaid and a README in the markdown format.`
2025-07-02T16:33:50.4580071Z   - `@coderabbitai help me debug CodeRabbit configuration file.`
